GVIF3 Deserializer

CXD4984ER-W

Preliminary

Description
The CXD4984ER-W is a GVIF3 (Gigabit Video InterFace 3) deserializer IC. It is suitable for automotive camera system and
automotive AV interface applications. It supports RAW 8 / 10 / 12 / 16 / 20 bits data or YCbCr (YUV) 8 bits data
transmission or RGB 24 bits data transmission up to 9.6 Gbps video rate, and it includes Aux interface (I2C) and GPIO
interface.
(Applications: Automotive Camera System / Automotive Entertainment / Infotainment)

Features
◆ GVIF3 (Gigabit Video InterFace 3) deserializer which has 4 serial inputs
◆ Up to 9.6 Gbps video rate
◆ Output format: RAW 8 / 10 / 12 / 16 / 20 bits or YCbCr422 (YUV422) 8 bits or RGB 24 bits
◆ MIPI D-PHY / C-PHY CSI-2 Interface (2 Port)
◆ Aux interface (I2C) (2 Port)
◆ GPIO interface
◆ Sync signal transmission to image sensor
◆ Merge function of multiple videos
◆ Support for shielded twisted-pair and coaxial cables
◆ Support for power over serial cable operation
◆ ＋1.1 V / 1.8 V / 1.8 V or 3.3 V Power Supply
◆ VQFN 64 pins package (9 mm × 9 mm)
◆ Functional Safety
◆ Automotive qualified part

1
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

Power Supply Voltage Power-on / off Sequence and Chip Enable Setup
There are three power supplies: 1.1 V, 1.8 V, IO (VDDIO).
There are no restrictions on the power-on / off sequence for 1.1 V, 1.8 V, and IO power supplies. However, the chip enable
signal must be input to CE pin so as to satisfy the following restrictions when power supplies are turned on. Make sure that
all pins voltage do not exceed the absolute maximum ratings.

CXD4984ER-W

Description of Functions and Operation 1
Overview
GVIF3 serializer and deserializer can transmit the high speed video signals the sync signals for image sensor and the low
speed Aux / GPIO signals over one differential shielded twisted-pair cable or coaxial cable.
GVIF3 serializers and deserializer are designed to use with the GVIF2 and GVIF3 chipset.

The high speed video signals can be transmitted from a serializer to a deserializer, and the sync signals for image sensor
can be transmitted from deserializer to serializer. The Aux / GPIO signals can be transmitted bi-directionally and
simultaneously.
The data transmission from a GVIF3 transmitter to a GVIF3 receiver is called “stream” in this specification. The direction of
the video data transmission is called “downstream” and the reverse direction is called “upstream”.
The data rate of a GVIF3 transmitter is fixed and can be selected by register.
The deserializer extracts the video data from the received GVIF2 or GVIF3 signals, recovers the video clock automatically
and outputs them.

Fig. 12 The Concept Figure of System

Some of GVIF3 devices have the GVIF3 transmitter port and receiver port, the daisy chain can be consisted by connecting
these ports to other GVIF2 and GVIF3 devices.

The link at the GVIF3 transmitter / receiver must be established normally for all transmissions to be valid

34
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

Video Transmission
Video Stream Multiplexing
Serializer can multiplex the input video data onto the video stream which is transmitted from upstream GVIF devices.
The video stream GVIFID and slots are assigned to each video stream which is transmitted from each GVIF3
transmitter.
Serializer transmits the video data from upstream to downstream via GVIF3 transmitter.

Video Stream Demultiplexing
By selecting the video stream GVIFID, deserializer can demultiplex the video stream from multiplexed video streams
which are received at each GVIF3 receiver and output the demultiplexed video stream.
When the video stream is demultiplexed, the total output data size is the same as the data size of the selected video
streams.
Deserializer transmits all video data from upstream which are received at GVIF3 receivers to downstream via GVIF3
transmitter.
By setting the GVIF3RX*_DROP_SOURCE_DATA_GVIFID_* registers and the DAISY_GVIF3TRX*_SELECT registers,
some of the video data can be deleted or selected from the video data which are transmitted to downstream.

Slot
Multiple signal channels are time-division multiplexed in the GVIF3 interface. The video signals are transmitted in the
high speed downstream channel of these channels. This channel is divided into slots. The each slot has the fixed
bandwidth of 30 Mbytes/s. The number of slots is varied depending on the speed setting of the GVIF3 port. For
example, the number of slots is 16 slots for 4.8 Gbps mode.
When the video input is the LVDS (OpenLDI) / eDP interface and the system clocks are input externally, a pixel data are
transmitted by 3 Bytes. 1 slot per 10 MHz pixel clock is needed. For example, 8 slots are needed for the transmission of
LVDS (OpenLDI) video signals at 80 MHz pixel clock rate.
When the system clocks are not input externally, 1 slot per 9 MHz pixel clock rate is needed.
When the video input is MIPI interface and the system clocks are input externally, 1 slot per 240 Mbps which is total data
rate of all lanes is needed. For example, 8 slots are needed for the transmission of 4 lanes data at 480Mbps/lane.
When the system clocks are not input externally, 1 slot per 216 Mbps which is total data rate of all lanes is needed.

Aux Port
For the Aux data transmission, the I2C interface is supported. As the Aux port is shared with all of streams, all of the Aux
interfaces must be the same in the GVIF3 devices which use the Aux port in the stream.

35
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

I2C Interface
When the I2C interface is used for the Aux port, SDA and SCL pins of all GVIF2 and GVIF3 devices whose I2C interface
is enabled are connected virtually. The multi master is not supported.
The electric characteristics conform to the NXP Semiconductors N.V I2C specification, I2C-bus specification and user
manual UM10204 Rev.6. The IOL of Fast-mode Plus is the same as one of Fast-mode. The pull-up resistor should be
set properly so that I2C specification is satisfied.

Serializer /
Deserializer

Serializer /
Deserializer

I2C

Fig. 13 Aux Port (I2C)
The Aux port connected to the I2C master device should be set the pseudo slave of Aux port by the
AUX_I2C_PSEUDO_MASTER_DISABLE register which disables the pseudo master of Aux port.
The Aux port connected to the I2C slave device should be set the pseudo master of Aux port by the
AUX_I2C_PSEUDO_SLAVE_DISABLE register which disables the pseudo slave of Aux port.
The Aux port (pseudo slave) which is accessed by the I2C master device adjusts the timing by the clock stretching in
order to ensure matching the timing with the I2C slave device. The Aux port (pseudo master) supports the clock
stretching by the I2C slave device to which the GVIF3 device accesses. When the clock stretching time excesses the
time which is set by the AUX_*_I2C_TIMEOUT register, it is regarded as the bus error, and the GVIF3 device resets the
status of the Aux data transmission. When the link is broken, it is also regarded as the bus error, and the GVIF3 device
resets the status of the Aux data transmission. In reset, the I2C master of GVIF3 device goes to the STOP condition first,
and it sends 9 clock pulses, and then it goes to the STOP condition again. The access during reset sequence is invalid
and NACK can be output. The wait time must be more than 1 ms after I2C communication error occurs.
When the registers which are for link establishment are changed through the Aux port, the link can be broken and the
access can be stopped, and then NACK can be output.
General call address is not supported.
Only one of Aux port should be enabled when there are multiple Aux ports of GVIF devices connected to the same I2C
master devices
The tSU;STA minimum value of Standard-mode on the pseudo master of the Aux port is 2.7 μs.
The pseudo slave of the Aux port performs bit level clock stretching, therefore the I2C master must support bit level clock
stretching.
The Aux port (pseudo slave) which is accessed by the I2C master device adjusts the timing by the clock stretching in
order to ensure matching the timing with the I2C slave device. Therefore, the tVD;DAT may be more than maximum
value as described in the I2C-bus specification and user manual UM10204 Rev.6. If the I2C slave device does not
support the clock stretching, the I2C slave device must support the access which the tVD;DAT is more than or equal to
maximum value (the tSU;DAT meets minimum value).
.

36
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

GPIO Port
The GVIF3 device can transmit low speed GPIO signals in all streams. Virtual GPIO bus is constructed in a daisy chain.
One of all connected GVIF2 and GVIF3 devices can drive the specified virtual GPIO bus.

SYNC Port
The master clock signal and frame sync signal, which are provided to image sensor, can be transmitted from a deserializer
to an adjacent serializer. The kinds of signals which can be transmitted depend on each device.
The master clock signal which is input to the deserializer can be divided by the MASTER_CLK_DIVISION_RATIO register
and transmitted. When the division ratio is set, the master clock frequency in FRAME_SYNC setup of the serializer should
be equal to the divided master clock frequency
SYNC_ENABLE register of the deserializer must be set before SYNC_ENABLE register of the serializer is set.

Register Access Interface
The register can be accessed through SDA0 pin and SCL0 pin. The register cannot be accessed through the shared pins
which are assigned for the SDA1 and SCL1 signals.
The slave address is set by I2CADR pin.
The register access interface does not use the clock stretching.
When the registers which are for link establishment are changed, the link can be broken and reset automatically. As the link
is broken, all transmissions are stopped.
General call address is not supported.

The register consists of multiple banks.
Each bank can be accessed when its bank number is set to the address 0xFF. For example, the register of Bank 2 can be
accessed when the value 0x02 is written in the address 0xFF.

The GVIF3 device which has no HDCP function does not have the registers of Bank 8 and Bank 9.
If the HDCP function is not used, there is no need to use the registers of Bank 8 and Bank 9.
When the registers of Bank 8 and Bank 9 are write-accessed (Write Stop), the next access must start after more than 5.5
ms from the write access. If the next access start within this waiting period, the I2C bus returns NACK.
Please refer to the application note about the details of Bank 8 and Bank 9.

37
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

Register Remote Access Function
The register of another connected GVIF2 and GVIF3 device in streams can be read and written by registers. Multiple
GVIF2 and GVIF3 devices in streams cannot execute the register remote access function simultaneously. The register
cannot be write-accessed from the register access interface and the register remote access function simultaneously.
When the registers which are for link establishment are changed through the register remote access, the link can be
broken and the register remote access can be stopped, and then there can be no notification in the
REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE register.

The time from the completion of write or read setting to the “ 1 ” assertion of the
REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE register is 0.4 ms for the point to point connection, + 0.15 ms for 1 stage
addition of daisy chain connection.
When a GVIF2 and GVIF3 device in streams execute the remote register access function and then another GVIF2 and
GVIF3 device in streams execute the remote register access function, the wait time of remote register access function must
be more than 0.5 ms × (Number of connected GVIF2 and GVIF3 devices in stream).
By the register remote access function, the register of only Bank 0 in GVIF2 device can be accessed from GVIF3 device or
the register of only Bank 0 in GVIF3 device can be accessed from GVIF2 device.
The register of all banks in GVIF3 device can be accessed from GVIF3 device.
The registers of Bank 8 and Bank 9 can be read-accessed only.

I2CADR Pin Setup
The slave address for the register access interface is determined by 7 bits. The MSB 3 bits of them are fixed value, “ 010 ”.
The LSB 4 bits of them should be set by I2CADR pin.
I2CADR pin should be set with registers as follows.

Fig. 14 I2CADR pin Setup

GVIFID Pin Setup
The GVIFID is used to identify the serializer and the deserializer. The GVIFID is 8 bits. The LSB 4 bits are the logical value
of GVIFID pin.
The GVIFID pin should be set by resistors same as I2CADR pin.

For the daisy chain connection, The LSB 4 bits of GVIFID should be set to the different value in GVIF devices which are
within the range of the video transmission, audio transmission, register remote access

The video stream GVIFID should be set by register. For the daisy chain connection, the video stream GVIFID should be set
to the different value in GVIF devices which are within the range of the video transmission.

CMOS Logic Interface
By applying 1.8 V or 3.3 V to VDDIO, CMOS logic interface for 1.8 V or 3.3 V are supported. All CMOS logic interface pins
are specified to have the same interface.

INTERRUPT Signal and Register
The interrupt notification is indicated by INTERRUPT signal and register. INTERRUPT signal can be assigned to
GENERAL_IO[*:0] pin.
The item which is output to INTERRUPT signal and register can be selected by registers. The logical value of INTERRUPT
signal and register can be cleared by registers.

Fig. 15 Relation among Error Status Monitor - * register, Interrupt Setup - * register
and INTERRUPT pin / register

MIPI Alliance Specification for D-PHY Version 2.1 compliant.

Only the continuous clock mode is supported. The ULPS is not supported.
Only unidirectional Data Lanes are supported.
The following formats are supported in MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 without the frame extended mode.
 RGB888 (Data Type : 24h)
 YCbCr422 (YUV) (Data Type: 1Eh)
 RAW8 (Data Type: 2Ah)
 RAW10 (Data Type: 2Bh)
 RAW12(Data Type: 2Ch)
 RAW16 (Data Type: 2Eh)
 RAW20 (Data Type: 2Fh)

Except for RAW10, the number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be even.
For RAW10, the number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be a multiple of 4.
The number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be same.

42
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between Frame Start and Packet Header must be more than 1 μs. The time interval
between Packet Footer and Packet Header must be more than 1 μs × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with
line-interleave format in deserializer). The time interval between Frame End and Frame Start must be more than 2 μs ×
(The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY DSI interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between V Sync End and Packet Header of Long Packet must be more than 1 μs.
The time interval between Packet Footer of Long Packet and Packet Header of Long Packet must be more than 1 μs ×
(The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer). The time interval between V
Sync Start and V Sync End must be more than 2 μs × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave
format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is LVDS (OpenLDI) interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between the edge of VSYNC signal and the rising edge of DE signal must be more
than 1 μs. The time interval between the falling to rising edge of DE signal must be more than 1 μs × (The number of
Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer). The time interval between the edge of VSYNC
signal must be more than 2 μs × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in deserializer is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface and the data rate exceeds 1500 Mbps /
Lane, Periodic HS Skew Calibration Burst may be required in video output of deserializer.
When the interface of video port in serializer is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface and serializer transmits the video stream
with the Frame Extended Mode, the time interval between Frame End and Packet Headers of the next Long Packet
must be more than 13 µs × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer) in
video input of serializer. Then Periodic HS Skew Calibration Burst will be inserted between Frame End and Frame Start
in video output of deserializer, but it may not be inserted depending on the timing of Frame End of each video stream.
When SYNC signal is transmitted in High Accuracy Mode and the input data of each serializer is synchronized, Periodic
HS Skew Calibration Burst will be inserted between Frame End and Frame Start.

For the continuous clock mode, the MIPI receiver device must be started up and activated before the deserializer starts
outputting the MIPI clock signal. The VIDEO_OUTPUT_ENABLE_* register must be set to “ 0 ” before the MIPI receiver
device is started up and activated, and then the VIDEO_OUTPUT_ENABLE_* register must be set to “ 1 ” after the MIPI
receiver device is started up and activated.

The VIDEO_OUTPUT_ENABLE_* register must be set to “ 1 ” after setting the registers related to video transmission,
and it must be set to “ 0 ” before changing the registers related to video transmission.

Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

MIPI D-PHY Global Operation Timing Parameter Setup
Global Operation Timing parameter should be set by registers to satisfy the following equations.
When MIPITX half rate mode is not used, or when only one sub port is used, Global Operation Timing parameter should
be set to the same value in sub ports of the same port.

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)
roundup( ): the function of rounding up digits after a decimal point.
MPX: 1 (when MIPITX half rate mode is not used), 2 (when MIPITX half rate mode is used)

MIPI Alliance Specification for C-PHY Version 1.2 compliant.
MIPI Alliance Specification for CSI-2 Version 2.1 compliant.
Only unidirectional Data Lanes are supported.
The following formats are supported in MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 without the frame extended mode.
 RGB888 (Data Type : 24h)
 YCbCr422 (YUV) (Data Type: 1Eh)
 RAW8 (Data Type: 2Ah)
 RAW10 (Data Type: 2Bh)
 RAW12(Data Type: 2Ch)
 RAW16 (Data Type: 2Eh)
 RAW20 (Data Type: 2Fh)

47
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

Except for RAW10, the number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be even.
For RAW10, the number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be a multiple of 4.
The number of data in line of the valid pixel region must be same.

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between Frame Start and Packet Header must be more than “ Packet Interval 1 ”
shown in table below. The time interval between Packet Footer and Packet Header must be more than “ Packet Interval
1 ” × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer). The time interval between
Frame End and Frame Start must be more than “ Packet Interval 1 ” × 2 × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing
with line-interleave format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY DSI interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between V Sync End and Packet Header of Long Packet must be more than “ Packet
Interval 1 ” shown in table below. The time interval between Packet Footer of Long Packet and Packet Header of Long
Packet must be more than “ Packet Interval 1 ” × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format
in deserializer). The time interval between V Sync Start and V Sync End must be more than “ Packet Interval 1 ” × 2 ×
(The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is LVDS (OpenLDI) interface, in video
input of serializer, the time interval between the edge of VSYNC signal and the rising edge of DE signal must be more
than “ Packet Interval 1 ” shown in table below. The time interval between the falling to rising edge of DE signal must be
more than “ Packet Interval 1 ” × (The number of Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer).
The time interval between the edge of VSYNC signal must be more than “ Packet Interval 1 ” × 2 × (The number of
Virtual Channel Multiplexing with line-interleave format in deserializer).

When the interface of video port in deserializer is MIPI C-PHY CSI-2 interface and the data rate exceeds 3000 Msps /
Lane, Calibration may be required in video output of deserializer.
"Packet Interval 1" shown in Table below is calculated with the minimum calibration length case, so the required packet
interval may increase depending on the calibration length requested by the connected MIPI C-PHY receiver. In this
case, it should be added the calibration length increased by the register setting to the "Packet Interval 1".

The MIPI_TX0_0_SELECT, MIPI_TX0_1_SELECT, MIPI_TX1_2_SELECT and MIPI_TX1_3_SELECT registers select
which sub ports of MIPI D-PHY transmitter are used.
The UNLOADER*_SELECT registers select which Unloaders are used.
The UNLOADER*_SELECT register of unused Unloaders should be set to “ 0 ”.
The UNLOADER*_GVIF3RX_PORT_SELECT registers select which GVIF3 receiver is connected to each Unloader.
The UNLOADER*_TARGET_GVIFID registers select one of the video streams which are input from GVIF3 receiver.
The MIPI_TX0_0_UNLOADER_SELECT, MIPI_TX0_1_UNLOADER_SELECT, MIPI_TX1_2_UNLOADER_SELECT and
MIPI_TX1_3_UNLOADER_SELECT registers select which Unloaders are connected to each sub port of MIPI D-PHY
Transmitter. Each of Unloaders can be connected to only one of sub ports.

MIPITX VCID SELECT Function
By setting the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0_ENABLE and
UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1_ENABLE registers, and by selecting Virtual Channel ID with the
UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0 and UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1 registers, the video data of
52
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

specified Virtual Channel ID (maximum 2 video data) can be extracted from the video stream which is selected at each
Unloader. When these settings are not set, Virtual Channel ID of video data is output as it is.
It is necessary that the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2
interface and the frame extended mode is used.
The UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_OVR_0_ENABLE register should be set to “ 0 ”.
The video data of Virtual Channel ID which is not selected are replaced with blank data.
When the video data is line-interleave format and the clock fixed mode of MIPI D-PHY Transmitter is used, the output
clock frequency can be lowered according to the amount of extracted video data.
When the video data is frame-interleave format and the clock fixed mode of MIPI D-PHY Transmitter is used, the output
clock frequency should be set according to the amount of original video data.

MIPITX VCID OVERRIDE Function
When only one video data of Virtual Channel ID is included in the video stream which is selected at each Unloader,
Virtual Channel ID can be overridden by setting the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_OVR_0_ENABLE register to “ 1 ”
and by selecting another Virtual Channel ID with the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0 register.
It is necessary that the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2
interface and the frame extended mode is used.
The UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0_ENABLE and UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1_ENABLE
registers should be set to “ 0 ”.
When Virtual Channel ID is overridden by the MIPITX VCID OVERRIDE Function, The ECC value in Packet Header
should be recalculated and replaced by setting the UNLOADER*_ECC_CRC_OVR_ENABLE register to “ 1 ”.

MIPITX VCID SELECT & OVERRIDE Function
By setting the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1_ENABLE registers to “ 1 ”, and by selecting Virtual Channel ID
with the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1, and by setting the UNLOADER*_ECC_CRC_OVR_ENABLE register
to “ 1 ”, and by setting the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_OVR_0_ENABLE register to “ 1 ”, and by selecting another
Virtual Channel ID with the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0 register, the video data of specified Virtual
Channel ID can be extracted from the video stream which is selected at each Unloader, and Virtual Channel ID can be
overridden.

MIPITX VCID SETUP Function
When the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is not MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface or the
frame extended mode is not used, the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_OVR_0_ENABLE register should be set to “ 1 ”,
and Virtual Channel ID of video data should be set by the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0 register.
When these settings are not set, Virtual Channel ID of video data is set to " 0000 ".
The UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0_ENABLE and UNLOADER*_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_1_ENABLE
registers should be set to “ 0 ”.
The UNLOADER*_ECC_CRC_OVR_ENABLE registers should be set to “ 1 ”.

53
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

MIPITX Extra Virtual Channel ID Override Mode
By using the Extra Virtual Channel ID Override Mode, and by selecting up to 2 Virtual Channel ID, up to 2 video data of
specified Virtual Channel ID can be extracted from the video stream which is selected at each Unloader, and up to 2
Virtual Channel ID can be overridden.
To use Extra Virtual Channel ID Override Mode, the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_EXTRA_VCID_OVR_MODE_ENABLE
register should be set to "1".
By setting UNLOADER*_MIPITX_EXTRA_VCID_OVR_*_ENABLE registers to “ 1 ”, and by selecting Virtual Channel ID
with the UNLOADER*_MIPITX_EXTRA_VCID_SELECT_*, and by setting the
UNLOADER*_MIPITX_EXTRA_VCID_OVERRIDE_*, the video data of specified Virtual Channel ID can be extracted
from the video stream which is selected, and Virtual Channel ID can be overridden.
This mode can be set at each Unloader.
When Virtual Channel ID is overridden by the Extra Virtual Channel ID Override Mode, The ECC value in Packet Header
should be recalculated and replaced by setting the UNLOADER*_ECC_CRC_OVR_ENABLE register to “ 1 ”.

MIPITX Clock Fixed Mode
When multiple Unloaders are selected for one sub port, the video streams of selected Unloaders are combined into one
video data with line-interleave format and output. (Virtual Channel Multiplexing)
The MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE register selects the clock fixed mode of MIPI D-PHY Transmitter.
The output clock frequency should be set by the MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE_ENABLE_0,
MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE_ENABLE_1, MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE and
MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE registers.
It is necessary that the output clock frequency is more than the frequency for the largest amount of video data which are
output from each sub port.
It is necessary that the interface of video port in serializer which transmits the video stream is MIPI D-PHY CSI-2
interface.
The data rate when the clock fixed mode of MIPI C-PHY Transmitter is calculated as following equation.
𝑀𝐼𝑃𝐼 𝐶- 𝑃𝐻𝑌 𝑑𝑎𝑡𝑎 𝑟𝑎𝑡𝑒 𝑀𝑠𝑝𝑠 / 𝐿𝑎𝑛𝑒

𝑀𝐼𝑃𝐼 𝐷- 𝑃𝐻𝑌 𝑑𝑎𝑡𝑎 𝑟𝑎𝑡𝑒 𝑀𝑏𝑝𝑠 / 𝐿𝑎𝑛𝑒
7 𝑠𝑦𝑚𝑏𝑜𝑙
𝑀𝐼𝑃𝐼 𝐷- 𝑃𝐻𝑌 𝑑𝑎𝑡𝑎 𝑙𝑎𝑛𝑒 𝑛𝑢𝑚𝑏𝑒𝑟
16 𝑏𝑖𝑡
𝑀𝐼𝑃𝐼 𝐶- 𝑃𝐻𝑌 𝑑𝑎𝑡𝑎 𝑙𝑎𝑛𝑒 𝑛𝑢𝑚𝑏𝑒𝑟

MIPITX Clock Regenerated Mode
When one Unloader is selected for one sub port, the video stream of selected Unloader is output from sub port.
The MIPI_TX*_CLK_FIXED_MODE register selects the clock regenerated mode of MIPI D-PHY Transmitter.
In Unloaders which are connected to each sub port, the MIPI_TX*_REFCLK_SELECT register selects Unloader which
has the largest amount of video data in video stream as the supply source of the reference clock for MIPI D-PHY
Transmitter.

MIPITX Half Rate Mode
The output clock frequency for Sub port 1 of Port 0 can be half of that for Sub port 0 of Port 0.
The output clock frequency for Sub port 3 of Port 1 can be half of that for Sub port 2 of Port 1.
The clock fixed mode should be set, and the half rate mode should be set by the
MIPI_TX*_HALFRATE_MODE_ENABLE, MIPI_TX0_1_HALFRATE_MODE_ENABLE and
MIPI_TX1_3_HALFRATE_MODE_ENABLE registers.

CXD4984ER-W

System Clock Input
For the daisy chain connection, the video signal must satisfy the following.
 When the video input is the LVDS (OpenLDI) / eDP interface: 1 slot per 9 MHz pixel clock
 When the video input is MIPI interface: 1 slot per 216 Mbps which is total data rate of all lanes

And the system clocks should be input externally to GVIF devices between serializer in most upstream side and
deserializer in most downstream side. When the serializer in most upstream side is CXD4963ER-W or CXD4963GG-W or
CXD4967ER-W or CXD4965ER-W and the GVIF device between the serializer in most upstream side and deserializer in
most downstream side is one deserializer and it is CXD4960ER-W or CXD4960GG-W or CXD4964ER-W or CXD4966ERW or CXD4984ER-W, the system clock input is not needed.

The example of 6-stage daisy chain is shown in the following figure.
The system clocks which are input externally to GVIF3 devices between serializer in most upstream side and deserializer
in most downstream side are f_sysclk1, f_sysclk2, f_sysclk3, f_sysclk4, respectively.
Each system clock must satisfy the following.
 19 MHz < f_sysclk1, f_sysclk2, f_sysclk3, f_sysclk4 ≤ 20 MHz
 Frequency accuracy of f_sysclk1、f_sysclk2、f_sysclk3、f_sysclk4 < 100ppm

The external system clock input mode is set by registers.
Once the external system clock input mode is set, CE pin should be input to low level and IC should be reset in order to
disable the external system clock input mode.

Fig. 18 The example of 6-stage Daisy Chain

Fig. 19 System Clock Input Circuit

Handling of Unused GVIF3 Port
When the serializer / deserializer of GVIF3 devices have both GVIF3 transmitter and GVIF3 receiver, GVIF3 receiver of the
serializer / deserializer in the most upstream side of the stream and GVIF3 transmitter of the serializer / deserializer in the
most downstream side of the stream must be disabled.
The serializer / deserializer monitors the status of the streams from upstream to downstream and the READY signal goes
to high level when the link is established normally among all of GVIF2 transmitters, GVIF2 receivers, GVIF3 transmitters
and GVIF3 receivers which are not disabled.
When both GVIF3 transmitter and GVIF3 receiver in a GVIF3 device are disabled, the READY signal goes to high level.
There are two ways to disable GVIF3 transmitter. One is that VDD11A_G3TX is connected to GND. The other one is that the
GVIF3TX0_ENABLE register value is set to “ 0 ”.
To disable GVIF3 receiver, the GVIF3RX*_ENABLE register value is set to “ 0 ”.

60
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

Frame Extended Mode
The video data transmission function can be extended by setting the frame extended mode in serializer.
In the frame extended mode, the packets of video signals which are input to serializer can be transmitted as it is and output
them from deserializer.
The deserializer works in the same mode as that which is selected in the serializer.

In the frame extended mode, the number of data in line can be varied for each line. In the normal mode, the number of data
in line of the valid pixel region must be constant.
In the frame extended mode, the Data Type shown in the table below can be transmitted. In the normal mode, only some of
Data Type are supported.

Table 8 Supported Data Type in Frame Extended Mode (MIPI D-PHY CSI-2)
Data Type
0x10 - 0x17
0x18 - 0x1F
0x20 - 0x27
0x28 - 0x2F
0x30 - 0x37
0x38 - 0x3F

Description
Generic 8-bit Long Packet Data Types
YUV Image Data Types
RGB Image Data Types
RAW Image Data Types
User Defined 8-bit Data Types
Reserved

Table 9 Supported Data Type in Frame Extended Mode (MIPI D-PHY DSI)
Data Type
0x09
0x19
0x2C
0x3E

Description
Null Packet, no data
Blanking Packet, no data
Packed Pixel Stream, 16-bit YCbCr, 4:2:2 Format
Packed Pixel Stream, 24-bit RGB, 8-8-8 Format

Fig. 21 The example of frame data which is supported in Frame Extended Mode (Left)
and Normal Mode (Right)

73
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

Detailed Description of Registers
The detailed description of each register is given below.
The upper, middle and lower of the table show the bit number, the register name and the read / write flag with the initial
value, respectively.
The “ ― ” means the reserved registers. The other addresses which are not described are also the reserved registers. Note
that they must not be changed from the initial value.
The register value “ 0 ” is defined as low level, and “ 1 ” as high level. “ x ” means the indeterminate value.
Do not set the values which are described “ Reserved ” in the detailed description of registers.

74
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

General Status Monitor - 1 : General status monitor 1

(bank0,0x00,R)

This register indicates the status of the GVIF3 device.

GVIF3TX
0_ACTIV
ATED
R-0

Bit7 : GVIF3RX1_ACTIVATED
This bit indicates the operating status of the GVIF3 receiver 1.
0: Idle
1: Initialization is completed and the link is established.
Bit4 : GVIF3RX0_ACTIVATED
This bit indicates the operating status of the GVIF3 receiver 0.
0: Idle
1: Initialization is completed and the link is established.
Bit0 : GVIF3TX0_ACTIVATED
This bit indicates the operating status of the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
0: Idle
1: Initialization is completed and the link is established.

Bit7 : INTERRUPT
This bit indicates the same logical value as INTERRUPT signal.
0: Low
1: High
Bit4 : READY
This bit indicates that unused GVIF port is disabled and the link is established normally among all of the
GVIF transmitters and GVIF receivers which are not disabled.
0: Port termination and link establishment are not completed.
1: Port termination and link establishment are completed.
Bit1 : GVIF3RX1_LOS
This bit indicates the signal reception status of the GVIF3 receiver 1.
0: Normal
1: Loss of signal
Bit0 : GVIF3RX0_LOS
This bit indicates the signal reception status of the GVIF3 receiver 0.
0: Normal
1: Loss of signal

This register can be cleared by the ERROR_CLEAR register.
The status of the GVIF3 device is changed and some errors may occur when other registers are set. This register must

RW-1

Bit7-4 : GVIF3TX0_SPEED
These bits set the data rate of serial output (downstream) of the GVIF3 transmitter 0. These bits should be
set according to the data rate setting in the GVIF*RX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected to
the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
When the upstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set after the data rate setting of the GVIF*RX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected
to the GVIF3 transmitter 0 is completed.
When the downstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set before the data rate setting of the GVIF*RX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is
connected to the GVIF3 transmitter 0 is completed.
0000 : Reserved
0001 : 2.4 Gbps
0010 : 3.6 Gbps
0011 : 4.8 Gbps
0100 : 6.0 Gbps
0101 : 7.2 Gbps
0110 : 8.4 Gbps
0111 : 9.6 Gbps
1000 : 10.8 Gbps
1001 : 12.0 Gbps
1010-1111 : Reserved
Bit3 : GVIF3TX0_FAIL_MASK_INTERVAL_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the error detection frequency setting of the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
0: Disable
1: Enable
Bit2 : GVIF3TX0_POL_INVERT
This bit sets the polarity of serial input / output pin of the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
When a coaxial cable is used, this bit must be set to " 0 ".
0: Not invert (the same as the pin name)
1: Invert
Bit0 : GVIF3TX0_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
0: Disable
1: Enable

103
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

Bit4-0 : GVIF3RX0_SPEED
These bits set the data rate of serial input (downstream) of the GVIF3 receiver 0. These bits should be set
according to the data rate setting in the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected to the
GVIF3 receiver 0.
When the downstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set after the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected
to the GVIF3 receiver 0 is completed.
When the upstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set before the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is
connected to the GVIF3 receiver 0 is completed.
00000: 2.4 Gbps, 3.6 Gbps, 4.8 Gbps
00001-10011: Reserved
10100: 6.0 Gbps
10101: 7.2 Gbps
10110: 8.4 Gbps
10111: 9.6 Gbps
11000: 10.8 Gbps
11001: 12.0 Gbps
11010-11111: Reserved

Bit7-0 : GVIF3TX0_FAIL_MASK_INTERVAL
These bits set the error detection frequency of the GVIF3 transmitter 0.
The GVIF3TX0_FAIL_MASK_INTERVAL_ENABLE register need to be set.
The value equal to or greater than 1 should be set.
READY can be " 0 " during the error masked period.
The error masked period is ( 50 ns +/- 10 % ) × 8 × GVIF3TX0_FAIL_MASK_INTERVAL.

Bit7-4 : REMOTE_REGISTER_TARGET_BANK
These bits set the register bank number which is remote-accessed by this GVIF3 device.
Bit1 : REMOTE_REGISTER_READ
This bit sets the read process.
When this register is changed from “ 0 ” to “ 1 ”, the read process is executed.
Bit0 : REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE
This bit sets the write process.
When this register is changed from “ 0 ” to “ 1 ”, the write process is executed.

PLETE

Bit1 : REMOTE_REGISTER_READ_COMPLETE
This bit indicates the completion of the read process.
When the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ register or REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE register is changed from
“ 0 ” to “ 1 ”, the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ_COMPLETE register and
REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE register are cleared once.
0: Not completed
1: Complete
Bit0 : REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE
This bit sets the completion of the write process.
When the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ register or REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE register is changed from
“ 0 ” to “ 1 ”, the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ_COMPLETE register and
REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE register are cleared once.
0: Not completed
1: Completed

<Write Procedure>
(1) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 5 register (0xE8).
(2) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 1 register (0xDF).
(3) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_TARGET_BANK register (0xE3, bit7-4).
(4) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 2 register (0xE0).
(5) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 3 register (0xE1).
(6) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE register (0xE3, bit0) to “ 1 ”.
(7) Confirm that the REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE_COMPLETE register (0xE4, bit0) is “ 1 ”.
(8) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_WRITE register (0xE3, bit0) to “ 0 ”.
(9) Go back to (1) of each procedure if the write or read procedure is continued.

<Read Procedure>
(1) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 5 register (0xE8).
(2) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 1 register (0xDF).
(3) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_TARGET_BANK register (0xE3, bit7-4).
(4) Set the Register Remote Access Setup - 2 register (0xE0).

137
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

CXD4984ER-W

(5) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ register (0xE3, bit1) to “ 1 ”.
(6) Confirm that the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ_COMPLETE register (0xE4, bit1) is “ 1 ”.
(7) Read data from the Register Remote Access Monitor - 1 register (0xE2).
(8) Set the REMOTE_REGISTER_READ register (0xE3, bit1) to “ 0 ”.
(9) Go back to (1) of each procedure if the write or read procedure is continued.

1: Set

1: Set

0: Not set
1: Set

Bit7-0 : MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2
These bits set the MSB 8 bits ([15:8]) of the PLL parameter of MIPI output (Port 0) with the clock fixed mode.
The value of the following equation should be set.

MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2[15] = 0
MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2[14:0] = fractional part of (DR × D / (System clock frequency))
× 2 ^ 15

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)

The system clock frequency is determined by the following.
External system clock input mode: the frequency of external system clock
Internal system clock mode: 20 (MHz)

The value of D is determined by the value of the MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE register.
0001-0011 : D=1
0100-0110 : D=2
0111-1001 : D=4
1010-1100 : D=8
1101-1111 : D=16

Bit7 : MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_ENABLE_0
This bit enables or disables the setting of the clock fixed mode of MIPI output (Port 0).
When the clock regeneration mode is set by the MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE register, this bit should be
set to " 0 ".
0: Disable
1: Enable
Bit2-0 : MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE
These bits set the MSB 3 bits ([10:8]) of the PLL parameter of MIPI output (Port 0) with the clock fixed mode.
The value of the following equation should be set. (Round down to the nearest integer.)

MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE = Integer part of (DR × D / (System clock frequency))

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)

The system clock frequency is determined by the following.
External system clock input mode: the frequency of external system clock
Internal system clock mode: 20 (MHz)

The value of D is determined by the value of the MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE register.
0001-0011 : D=1
0100-0110 : D=2
0111-1001 : D=4
1010-1100 : D=8
1101-1111 : D=16

When the internal system clock is used, the actual MIPI D-PHY data rate is the value of the following
equation.
maximum : DR × (21 / 20) × ((100 + maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)
minimum : DR × ((100 - maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)

When the external system clock is used, the actual MIPI D-PHY data rate is the value of the following
equation.

173

maximum : DR ×((100 + maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)
minimum : DR × ((100 - maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)

Bit3-0 : MIPI_TX0_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE
These bits set the frequency range of MIPI output (Port 0) with the clock fixed mode.

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)

0000: Reserved
0001: 3600 Mbps < DR ≤ 4500 Mbps
0010: 2850 Mbps < DR ≤ 3600 Mbps
0011: 2275 Mbps < DR ≤ 2850 Mbps
0100: 1800 Mbps < DR ≤ 2275 Mbps
0101: 1425 Mbps < DR ≤ 1800 Mbps
0110: 1137.5 Mbps < DR ≤ 1425 Mbps
0111: 900 Mbps < DR ≤ 1137.5 Mbps
1000: 712.5 Mbps < DR ≤ 900 Mbps

Bit2 : SSCG_0_SPREAD_RATE
These bits set the MSB 1 bits ([8:8]) of the spread rate of SSCG.
0 0001 1110: maximum spread rate of SSCG +/- 0.25 % (Center Spread)
0 0101 0000: maximum spread rate of SSCG +/- 0.5 % (Center Spread)
0 1010 0000: maximum spread rate of SSCG +/- 1.0 % (Center Spread)
0 1111 0000: maximum spread rate of SSCG +/- 1.5 % (Center Spread)
1 0100 0000: maximum spread rate of SSCG +/- 2.0 % (Center Spread)
Others: Reserved
Bit1-0 : SSCG_0_MODULATION_FREQ
These bits set the MSB 2 bits ([9:8]) of the modulation frequency of SSCG.
When it is DR ≤ 2500 Mbps in the GVIF3 deserializer which has MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface or when the
GVIF3 deserializer which has other video interface except MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface:
11 1110 1000: 10 kHz
10 1001 1011: 15 kHz
Others : Reserved

When it is DR > 2500 Mbps in the GVIF3 deserializer which has MIPI D-PHY CSI-2 interface:
01 0011 0110: 30 to 33 kHz (using external system clock input mode (19 MHz ≤ frequency < 20 MHz))
01 0100 0110: 30 to 33 kHz (using external system clock input mode (20 MHz ≤ frequency ≤ 21 MHz) or
using internal system clock mode)
Others : Reserved

Bit7-0 : GVIF3RX0_EQ_MODE
These bits set EQ parameter according to the serial cable type and data rate which is used for the GVIF3
receiver 0.
After these bits are changed, the GVIF3RX0_ENABLE register must be set to " 0 " and then it must be set to
" 1 ".
0100 0000: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX0_SPEED register setting
8.4 to 12.0 Gbps (Low Gain Mode. This setting lowers the maximum limit of equalizer gain.)
1010 1111: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX0_SPEED register setting 2.4 to 3.6 Gbps
1010 1101: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX0_SPEED register setting 4.8 to 7.2 Gbps
1101 1101: STP cable, the GVIF3RX0_SPEED register setting 8.4 to 9.6 Gbps
1111 1011: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX0_SPEED register setting
2.4 to 7.2 Gbps (Default)

These bits set the module number of Unloader which is connected to sub port 1 of the video data output.
Each of the Unloaders can be connected to only one of sub ports.
The bit number indicates the module number of Unloader. The corresponding bits should be set to " 1 " to
select the Unloaders.
Bit0: Unloader 0
Bit1: Unloader 1
Bit2: Unloader 2
Bit3: Unloader 3
Bit4: Unloader 4 (CXD4964ER-W and CXD4984ER-W only)
Bit5: Unloader 5 (CXD4964ER-W and CXD4984ER-W only)
Bit6: Unloader 6 (CXD4964ER-W and CXD4984ER-W only)
Bit7: Unloader 7 (CXD4964ER-W and CXD4984ER-W only)

Bit3 : GVIFID_GVIF3RX1_EXOR_OVR_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the setting which convert the LSB 2 bits of GVIFID (video stream GVIFID) in
serializer to the EXOR logical operated value between the LSB 2 bits of GVIFID (video stream GVIFID) in
serializer and the 2 bits of the port number of GVIF3 receiver.
CXD4963GG-W or CXD4963ER-W or CXD4961ER-W should be connected to GVIF3 receiver by the point
to point connection.
When this bit is set to " 1 ", the converted video stream GVIFID should be used to specify the video stream
GVIFID after GVIF3 receiver.
0: Disable
1: Enable

Bit4-0 : GVIF3RX1_SPEED
These bits set the data rate of serial input (downstream) of the GVIF3 receiver 1. These bits should be set
according to the data rate setting in the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected to the
GVIF3 receiver 1.
When the downstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set after the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected
to the GVIF3 receiver 1 is completed.
When the upstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set before the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is
connected to the GVIF3 receiver 1 is completed.
00000: 2.4 Gbps, 3.6 Gbps, 4.8 Gbps
00001-10011: Reserved
10100: 6.0 Gbps
10101: 7.2 Gbps
10110: 8.4 Gbps
10111: 9.6 Gbps
11000: 10.8 Gbps
11001: 12.0 Gbps
11010-11111: Reserved

UNLOADER3_MIPITX_VCID_SELECT_0 register.
When this bit is not enabled, the received data of all Virtual Channel ID is output.
0: Disable the output setting of Virtual Channel ID
1: Enable the output setting of Virtual Channel ID
Bit2 : UNLOADER3_MIPITX_VCID_OVR_0_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the override-setting of Virtual Channel ID number in the Unloader 3.
0: Disable
1: Enable

Bit7-0 : GVIF3RX1_EQ_MODE
These bits set EQ parameter according to the serial cable type and data rate which is used for the GVIF3
receiver 1.
After these bits are changed, the GVIF3RX1_ENABLE register must be set to " 0 " and then it must be set to
" 1 ".
0100 0000: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX1_SPEED register setting
8.4 to 12.0 Gbps (Low Gain Mode. This setting lowers the maximum limit of equalizer gain.)
1010 1111: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX1_SPEED register setting 2.4 to 3.6 Gbps
1010 1101: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX1_SPEED register setting 4.8 to 7.2 Gbps
1101 1101: STP cable, the GVIF3RX1_SPEED register setting 8.4 to 9.6 Gbps
1111 1011: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX1_SPEED register setting
2.4 to 7.2 Gbps (Default)

Bit7-0 : MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2
These bits set the MSB 8 bits ([15:8]) of the PLL parameter of MIPI output (Port 1) with the clock fixed mode.
The value of the following equation should be set.

MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2[15] = 0
MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE2[14:0] = fractional part of (DR x D / (System clock frequency))
× 2 ^ 15

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)

The system clock frequency is determined by the following.
External system clock input mode: the frequency of external system clock
Internal system clock mode: 20 (MHz)

The value of D is determined by the value of the MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE register.
0001-0011 : D=1
0100-0110 : D=2
0111-1001 : D=4
1010-1100 : D=8
1101-1111 : D=16

Bit7 : MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_ENABLE_0
This bit enables or disables the setting of the clock fixed mode of MIPI output (Port 1).

set to " 0 ".
0: Disable
1: Enable
Bit2-0 : MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE
These bits set the MSB 3 bits ([10:8]) of the PLL parameter of MIPI output (Port 1) with the clock fixed mode.
The value of the following equation should be set. (Round down to the nearest integer.)

MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_PLL_VALUE = Integer part of (DR × D / (System clock frequency))

DR: MIPI D-PHY data rate (Mbps / Lane)

The system clock frequency is determined by the following.
External system clock input mode: the frequency of external system clock
Internal system clock mode: 20 (MHz)

The value of D is determined by the value of the MIPI_TX1_CLK_FIXED_MODE_FREQ_RANGE register.
0001-0011 : D=1
0100-0110 : D=2
0111-1001 : D=4
1010-1100 : D=8
1101-1111 : D=16

When the internal system clock is used, the actual MIPI D-PHY data rate is the value of the following
equation.
Maximum : DR × (21 / 20) × ((100 + maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)
Minimum : DR × ((100 - maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)

When the external system clock is used, the actual MIPI D-PHY data rate is the value of the following
equation.

Minimum : DR × ((100 - maximum spread rate of SSCG(%)) / 100)

Bit4-0 : GVIF3RX2_SPEED
These bits set the data rate of serial input (downstream) of the GVIF3 receiver 2. These bits should be set
according to the data rate setting in the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected to the
GVIF3 receiver 2.
When the downstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set after the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected
to the GVIF3 receiver 2 is completed.
When the upstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set before the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is
connected to the GVIF3 receiver 2 is completed.
00000: 2.4 Gbps, 3.6 Gbps, 4.8 Gbps
00001-10011: Reserved
10100: 6.0 Gbps
10101: 7.2 Gbps
10110: 8.4 Gbps
10111: 9.6 Gbps

Bit3 : GVIFID_GVIF3RX3_EXOR_OVR_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the setting which convert the LSB 2 bits of GVIFID (video stream GVIFID) in
serializer to the EXOR logical operated value between the LSB 2 bits of GVIFID (video stream GVIFID) in
serializer and the 2 bits of the port number of GVIF3 receiver.

to point connection.

GVIFID after GVIF3 receiver.

Bit4-0 : GVIF3RX3_SPEED
These bits set the data rate of serial input (downstream) of the GVIF3 receiver 3. These bits should be set
according to the data rate setting in the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected to the
GVIF3 receiver 3.
When the downstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set after the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is connected
to the GVIF3 receiver 3 is completed.
When the upstream GVIF device changes these bits with the register remote access function, these bits
should be set before the data rate setting of the GVIF*TX*_SPEED register in GVIF device which is
connected to the GVIF3 receiver 3 is completed.
00000: 2.4 Gbps, 3.6 Gbps, 4.8 Gbps
00001-10011: Reserved
10100: 6.0 Gbps
10101: 7.2 Gbps
10110: 8.4 Gbps
10111: 9.6 Gbps
11000: 10.8 Gbps
11001: 12.0 Gbps
11010-11111: Reserved

These bits set the port number of GVIF3 receiver to be connected to the Unloader 6.

This bit enables or disables the ECC/CRC recalculation of the input video data which is stored in the
Unloader 6.

be set to " 1 " prior to setting the VIDEO_OUTPUT_ENABLE_* register to " 1 ".
0: Disable
1: Enable

This bit sets the mute of the input video data which is stored in the Unloader 6.
When the mute turns on, the black screen is transmitted instead of the input video data.
0: Mute OFF
1: Mute ON
Bit0 : UNLOADER6_SELECT
This bit enables or disables the Unloader 6.
0: Disable
1: Enable

1

0

RW-1

RW-1

Bit7-0 : GVIF3RX2_EQ_MODE
These bits set EQ parameter according to the serial cable type and data rate which is used for the GVIF3
receiver 2.
After these bits are changed, the GVIF3RX2_ENABLE register must be set to " 0 " and then it must be set to
" 1 ".
0100 0000: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX2_SPEED register setting
8.4 to 12.0 Gbps (Low Gain Mode. This setting lowers the maximum limit of equalizer gain.)
1010 1111: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX2_SPEED register setting 2.4 to 3.6 Gbps
1010 1101: COAX cable, the GVIF3RX2_SPEED register setting 4.8 to 7.2 Gbps
1101 1101: STP cable, the GVIF3RX2_SPEED register setting 8.4 to 9.6 Gbps
1111 1011: STP cable, Intra/Inter-board differential connection, the GVIF3RX2_SPEED register setting
2.4 to 7.2 Gbps (Default)

Bit7-6 : AUX_1_I2C_SPEED_MODE
These bits set the data rate of the Aux data transmission (I2C) which is assigned for shared pins. (Port 1)
00: Standard-mode (Max. 100 kbps)
01: Fast-mode (Max. 400 kbps)
10: Fast-mode Plus (Max. 1 Mbps)
11: Reserved
Bit0 : AUX_1_I2C_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables the Aux data transmission (I2C) which is assigned for shared pins. (Port 1)
This bit must be set after the signal assignment (the Shared Pin Setup - * register) is set.
This bit must be set to " 1 " after setting other registers of the Aux1 Setup - * registers, and it must be set to "
0 " before changing other registers of the Aux1 Setup - * registers.
0: Disable
1: Enable

Bit2 : MIPI_TX0_CPHY_MIRROR_MODE
This bit enables or disables the mirroring between the Sub port 0 and Sub port 1 of MIPI C-PHY output (Port
0). The Sub port 1 outputs the same data as Sub port 0.
0: Disable
1: Enable
The mirroring can be used when MIPI_TX0_CPHY_DATA_MODE is set to C-PHY Data Mode 1. The number
of data transmission lanes can be set to 1 for C-PHY.
Bit1-0 : MIPI_TX0_CPHY_DATA_MODE
This bit sets the assignment of the data lane. Please refer to the description of functions and operation. (Port
0)
00 : Reserved
01 : Reserved
10 : C-PHY Data Mode 0
11 : C-PHY Data Mode 1

332
Preliminary Rev.A0.2

For Desay

Bit5 : MIPI_TX0_CPHY_DATA_LANE3_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables MIPI C-PHY Data Lane 3 (Sub port 0).
If the number of the used lanes of sub port 0 is 2 or less, "0" should be set.
0 : Disable
1 : Enable
Bit4 : MIPI_TX0_CPHY_DATA_LANE2_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables MIPI C-PHY Data Lane 2 (Sub port 0).
If the number of the used lanes of sub port 0 is 1 or less, "0" should be set.
0 : Disable
1 : Enable

Bit2 : MIPI_TX1_CPHY_MIRROR_MODE
This bit enables or disables the mirroring between the Sub port 2 and Sub port 3 of MIPI C-PHY output (Port
1). The Sub port 3 outputs the same data as Sub port 2.
0: Disable
1: Enable
The mirroring can be used when MIPI_TX0_CPHY_DATA_MODE is set to C-PHY Data Mode 1. The number
of data transmission lanes can be set to 1 for C-PHY.
Bit1-0 : MIPI_TX1_CPHY_DATA_MODE
This bit sets the assignment of the data lane. Please refer to the description of functions and operation. (Port
1)
00 : Reserved
01 : Reserved
10 : C-PHY Data Mode 0
11 : C-PHY Data Mode 1

Bit5 : MIPI_TX1_CPHY_DATA_LANE3_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables MIPI C-PHY Data Lane 3 (Sub port 2).
If the number of the used lanes of sub port 0 is 2 or less, "0" should be set.
0 : Disable
1 : Enable
Bit4 : MIPI_TX1_CPHY_DATA_LANE2_ENABLE
This bit enables or disables MIPI C-PHY Data Lane 2 (Sub port 2).
If the number of the used lanes of sub port 0 is 1 or less, "0" should be set.
0 : Disable
1 : Enable
